%%\tagged{Ans@ShortAns, Type@Compute, Topic@Integral, Sub@Improper, Func@Radiucal, File@0071}{
\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0071. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{-3}^{16}{{-\frac{2}{\sqrt{-x + 16}}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0071.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{-3}^{16}{{-\frac{2}{\sqrt{-x + 16}}}\;dx} = \answer{-4 \, \sqrt{19}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{5}^{81}{{\frac{7}{\sqrt{-x + 81}}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0071.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{5}^{81}{{\frac{7}{\sqrt{-x + 81}}}\;dx} = \answer{28 \, \sqrt{19}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{

\end{multipleChoice}

\int_{-7}^{25}{{-\frac{7}{\sqrt{-x + 25}}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0071.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{-7}^{25}{{-\frac{7}{\sqrt{-x + 25}}}\;dx} = \answer{-56 \, \sqrt{2}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\int_{-7}^{9}{{-\frac{6}{\sqrt{-x + 9}}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0071.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{-7}^{9}{{-\frac{6}{\sqrt{-x + 9}}}\;dx} = \answer{-48}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0071. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{6}^{9}{{\frac{3}{\sqrt{-x + 9}}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0071.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{6}^{9}{{\frac{3}{\sqrt{-x + 9}}}\;dx} = \answer{6 \, \sqrt{3}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}
